                     <orth orig="Bu" lang="ar">عَظُمَ</orth>

                  <foreign lang="ar">كَبُرَ</foreign>, (S, TA,) said of a thing [as meaning <hi rend="ital">it was,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">became, great, big,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">large</hi>], (S, Msb, TA,) <hi rend="ital">in length</hi> and <hi rend="ital">breadth</hi> and <hi rend="ital">thickness:</hi> (TA:) [and in like manner, metaphorically, said of an object of intellect; meaning <hi rend="ital">it was,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">became, great in estimation</hi> or <hi rend="ital">rank</hi> or <hi rend="ital">dignity;</hi> and thus also said of a man: or it imports more than <foreign lang="ar">كَبُرَ</foreign>; signifying <hi rend="ital">it was,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">became, great in comparison with other things of its kind; huge, enormous,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">vast;</hi> and in a similar sense it is said of a man; and in an incomparably higher sense, of God: (see <foreign lang="ar">عَظِيمٌ</foreign>, below:)] and   
      <foreign lang="ar"> <ref cref="n29667-1" target="اعظم" n="1" type="1" subtype="WO" lang="ar" select="n29669"/></foreign> said of an affair, or event, signifies [like <foreign lang="ar">عَظُمَ</foreign>] <hi rend="ital">it became</hi>

      <foreign lang="ar"> <ref cref="n29690-3" target="عُظْمٌ" n="3" type="1" subtype="WO" lang="ar" select="n29674"/></foreign>, it is said, [as also <foreign lang="ar">مُعْظَمٌ</foreign> in many cases,] signifies the <hi rend="ital">middle,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">midst,</hi> of a thing. (TA.) It is said in a trad. of Ibn-Seereen, <foreign lang="ar">جَلَسْتُ إِلَى مَجْلِسٍ فِيهِ <ref cref="n29690-4" target="عُظْمٌ" n="4" type="5" subtype="FSO" lang="ar" select="n29674"/>مِنَ الأَنْصَارِ</foreign>, meaning [<hi rend="ital">I sat by an assembly in which was</hi>] <hi rend="ital">a numerous company of the Ansár.</hi> (TA.) [<foreign lang="ar">مُعْظَمُ</foreign> 
                  <foreign lang="ar">الحَرْبِ</foreign>, and <foreign lang="ar">المَوْتِ</foreign>, signify <hi rend="ital">The thick,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">thickest,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">the main stress</hi> or <hi rend="ital">struggle, of the fight</hi> or <hi rend="ital">battle,</hi> and <hi rend="ital">of death</hi> in battle: see <foreign lang="ar">رَحًى</foreign> (near the end of the paragraph) in art. <foreign lang="ar">رحو</foreign> and <foreign lang="ar">رحى</foreign>.]          <sense type="b" n="2">-b2-</sense>  [And accord. to Freytag, it occurs in the Deewan of the Hudhalees as signifying The <hi rend="ital">harder parts of the body,</hi> as the <hi rend="ital">neck,</hi> the <hi rend="ital">thigh,</hi> &amp;c.]          <sense type="b" n="3">-b3-</sense>  See also <foreign lang="ar">عَظِيمٌ</foreign>:          <sense type="b" n="4">-b4-</sense>  and <foreign lang="ar">عَظِيمَةٌ</foreign>.
